properties ^zx0igTQP

if A is singular ⟶ rank(A)<n ^45bRDax8

Rouche-Capelli theorem ^HgwgZAO6

system of n linear equations ^CIXUQnZO

has solution IFF ^6x3Cz3xR

rank(A)=rank(A|b) ^GFSpLj5Q

rank(A)=n ⟶ unique solution ^Mg0nysl7

null space ^F5eM6mis

N(A) ^H6d2ix1U

Example ^kiY3MLKZ
